915 : OJO 71 (1181) vo 11 |OJO 71 (1181) vo 11: saṅhapĕn iṅ wuhaya awuka tan tĕmwasana liputĕn iṅ dhīra wulaṅun ... Goris (index) says: ``phira (Skt., but not in PW) snake''. Based on what information? KBW s.v.) phira: ``to be read dhīra in the sense of ocean?'' MW gives under dhīra: the ocean, sea (as an image of constancy?), but gives no reference. The use of liputĕn and saputĕn makes the interpretation of Goris very improbable. The fact that phira occurs six times and is such a rare word makes it unlikely that phira in the texts stands for dhīra. In similar curse#formulas we find liputĕn connected with agni (liputĕn gĕsĕṅana de saṅ hyaṅ agni): VG VII 32 f. (860) XI.a;  phira II
